**python_mutable_default_arg** [python]
Python mutable default: list/dict default is shared across all calls — use None and create inside

W: def func(items=[]): items.append(x) — the default list is created once and shared.
C: def func(items=None): if items is None: items = [].

**python_late_binding_closure** [python]
Python late binding: lambda in loop captures variable by reference — use default arg to bind value early
T: "all my lambdas return the same value from the loop"  "closure in for loop always uses last value"
W: [lambda: i for i in range(5)] — all lambdas capture the variable i, returning its final value.
C: use a default argument: [lambda i=i: i for i in range(5)].
